Hirota's Policy Towards China 35

Seeking Sino-Japanese "Manchukuo" Cooperation: Suma Returns with New Instructions

Nanjing: The international situation after the breakdown of the disarmament conference seems superficially calm, but future trade relations may inevitably deteriorate considerably. Therefore, Foreign Minister Hirota is seeking to prevent any shaking of the foundation between China, Japan, and Manchukuo, and is focusing on the realization of East Asian policy. Ambassador Yoshizawa has instructed Suma, the Consul General in Nanjing, to return to Japan in early February. In mid-February, Ambassador Arita will go to China to succeed him. Taking this opportunity, the diplomatic organs in China will be refreshed, and the following new policies will be pursued to increase the mutual welfare of the Chinese and Japanese people and move towards a long-term plan: 1. If Sino-Japanese relations reach a state of possible cooperation, provide all assistance for China's independence and prosperity. 2. The fundamental reason for the Chinese people's self-reliance lies in the cultivation of the people's strength. Therefore, it is necessary to stabilize politics. 3. To prevent disasters, water conservancy projects should be prioritized. Therefore, major companies such as the South Manchuria Railway will be used as intermediaries to establish Sino-Japanese joint ventures, respecting the existing rights and interests of foreign countries to prevent the deterioration of international relations. (19th Telecommunications Dispatch)

Kobe: Suma, the Consul General stationed in Nanjing, who is carrying important instructions from Foreign Minister Hirota and is hurrying back to Japan, departed from Kobe for Shanghai aboard the Nagasaki Maru at 11:00 AM on the 19th. (19th Allied Dispatch)

Japanese Parliament to Reconvene Tomorrow: Dissolution Inevitable; Government to Issue Statement 36

Nanjing: The government believes that the most strategically appropriate time to dissolve parliament is after the Prime Minister, Foreign Minister, and Finance Minister have delivered speeches outlining their policy directions. It is now devising various plans to strike decisively. At the same time, it believes that the reasons for the dissolution must be made known to the people as a whole. Therefore, it plans to issue a statement regarding the dissolution of parliament in the form of a conversation by Prime Minister Okada after the dissolution. The original draft is currently being carefully prepared by Chief Secretary Shirane. The gist of its content is roughly as follows: Under the current domestic and international situation, the government has consistently acted in the spirit of national unity. However, the current political situation cannot be expected to lead to satisfactory progress in national affairs. Therefore, the government has respectfully requested an imperial edict to dissolve the House of Representatives and inform the people. However, the government hopes to hold fair general elections and make every effort to promote the progress of the nation. (19th Allied Dispatch)

Various Political Parties Convene General Meetings 37

Nanjing: The 68th session of parliament, fraught with the possibility of dissolution, will reconvene on the 21st. Various political parties have decided to convene party congresses on the 20th beforehand to prepare for the upcoming dissolution. It has been decided that political parties will submit an all-encompassing vote of no confidence to confront the government head-on. The Seiyukai will convene a congress at its headquarters at 2:00 PM on the 20th, with a high spirit of not fearing dissolution and aligning its steps. The government and the party have always advocated dissolution. The Minseito will also convene a congress at Seiyoken in Ueno at 1:00 PM on the same day. The Kokumin Domei will also hold a meeting on this day. These gatherings are largely demonstrations for general elections after dissolution, so the procedures for the general election have already been prepared, and the situation is quite tense. (19th Allied Dispatch)

Tokyo: The Seiyukai held a temporary plenary session of internal and external affairs at the Kyo San Entei yesterday afternoon to discuss the three methods proposed at the previous general affairs meeting: 1. Adopt the plan of collectively clarifying the principles and individually appealing to the Emperor? 2. Submit an all-encompassing vote of no confidence? 3. Submit both plans together? The debate was chaotic and inconclusive. It recessed at 6:00 PM and reconvened at 9:00 PM, but the dispute continued. General Affairs Director Kuhara then proposed that the general affairs meeting on the 19th discuss the issue, and the meeting adjourned at 12:20 AM. However, the general trend of the party is largely inclined to submit an all-encompassing vote of no confidence including the clarification of national principles at the beginning of parliament. (19th Telecommunications Dispatch)

Composition of Questions in the House of Peers 38

Tokyo: The 68th session of parliament will reconvene on the 21st. The House of Peers has decided on the procedure for questioning the ministers of state by lottery on the 18th as follows: 1. Katō Masanosuke will question the Prime Minister, Minister of Agriculture and Forestry, and Minister of the Navy regarding fisheries policy. 2. Baron Taguchi Takehiko will question the Minister of Education regarding the concept of national polity and educational policy. 3. Aoki Saijirō will question the Prime Minister, Minister of the Interior, Minister of the Army, and Minister of the Navy regarding the purification of elections and the promotion of the Japanese spirit. 4. Baron Sakamoto Toshiatsu will question the Prime Minister regarding the London Conference and national defense issues. 5. Baron Ki Toshihide will question the Prime Minister and Minister of Education regarding the promotion of national education. (19th Allied Dispatch)

Key Points of Hirota's Diplomatic Speech 39

Tokyo: Foreign Minister Hirota has decided to deliver a speech outlining diplomatic policy at the beginning of the reconvened parliament. The key points are recorded below: 1. The Japanese government believes that maintaining and ensuring free trade policies is the most effective way to promote world peace. It has always taken the lead and consistently followed the principles of free trade. The entire territory of Japan has historically allowed the free flow of people and goods from all countries around the world, and this remains the case today. 2. However, looking directly at the current world situation, on the one hand, inexpensive and high-quality Japanese goods are blocked by unfair tariff barriers in various countries. On the other hand, the overseas advancement of the Japanese people is also effectively prohibited worldwide. 3. The Japanese government believes that such trade measures are the greatest fundamental obstacle to maintaining world peace. It should demand from the world the indispensable conditions for national survival, namely, the free flow of people and goods, and request the opening of world markets and resources. All countries should guarantee Japan's peaceful progress in the world. (19th Allied Dispatch)

Fage Speaks on the Position Regarding the Naval Disarmament Conference; Failure of the Five-Power Conference Due to Political Issues; Japanese Delegation to Return Home Via the United States 40

Paris: Naval Minister Pietri recently gave an interview to Le Petit Parisien regarding the situation at the naval conference, stating that the failure of the five-nation conference was due to political issues interfering. He said, "Each country has the right to determine what naval forces are needed to maintain its own security. However, six months before the implementation of the annual shipbuilding program, other countries should be notified with necessary and clear information. If this is the case, the situation of naval issues can be clearly understood. After the naval conference is over, we can leave London without fear of repeating the absurd dangers of naval competition. All naval powers either secretly build ships or suddenly build ships, which are nothing more than the steps of such competition. When the naval conference reconvened at the beginning of this month, our delegation proposed the above suggestions, and the delegations of other countries praised them in unison. At that time, I felt that Japan could also agree. However, the Japanese delegation insisted that the naval conference must make a decision on the joint maximum amount proposed by that country, which led to the failure of the matter. If the Japanese did not know that the joint maximum amount could cause the failure of the naval conference, why did they still propose this proposal? It must be due to political reasons, which France wanted to avoid. France knew that quantitative restrictions were not the only issue that should be discussed at the naval conference, nor were they the only important issue, but it still insisted on discussing this first. As for the humanization of submarine warfare, France has the strongest submarine force among all countries, so it has a direct interest in it. However, we should be clear that submarine warfare should still be controlled by military purposes. Moreover, compared with its national defense needs, France's battleship tonnage is still insufficient. In fact, France's protected interests are all over the world, its coastline is very long, and its distance from various colonies is also far, so it must maintain a considerable naval force." (19th Havas)

London: Members of the Japanese Plenipotentiary Delegation, Colonels Abe and Inagaki, and Lieutenant Colonel Nishida, are scheduled to return home via the United States on the Aeropa on the 25th of this month from Southampton. (18th Allied Dispatch)

Former British Foreign Secretary Hoare Likely to Succeed Long as First Lord of the Admiralty 41

London: Rumors are circulating that former Foreign Secretary Hoare will succeed Monsell as First Lord of the Admiralty after the London Naval Conference ends. Hoare's secretary refused to confirm these rumors today, but admitted that Hoare's name had been mentioned, but the authorities had not formally notified him. Hoare is still in Switzerland. (18th Reuters)

US Purchases Silver from Mexico 42

Mexico City: Finance Minister Suárez of Mexico City discussed silver issues with US Treasury Secretary Morgenthau at the beginning of this month. After returning home, it is now widely rumored that the Mexican government has agreed with the United States to reissue the Peso silver coin (containing 72% silver), which had been suspended due to the rise in silver prices. It is also reported that the United States has agreed to purchase approximately 60 million ounces of silver from Mexico at New York market prices. The Mexican government has begun to purchase newly mined raw silver from domestic silver mines, offering the New York market price for that day, but deducting a commission of 0.125%. (18th Havas)

Commentary

The Neglected Issue of Inner Mongolia 43

— Year

Recent domestic and foreign telegrams have reported serious incidents occurring between Bangjiang and Jining (Pingdiquan). Although the specific facts are difficult to ascertain, at a time when the nation is focused on the negotiations in eastern Hebei and northern Chahar, such warnings from Inner Mongolia cannot help but cause us great anxiety, given the past activities of ambitious nations in Mongolia.

Our anxiety stems from two points: 1. The so-called Inner Mongolia is a territory of China, and from east to west, it has close relations with nine provinces, including Liaoning, Heilongjiang, Jehol, Chahar, Suiyuan, Shanxi, Shaanxi, Gansu, and Ningxia. Today, apart from Liaoning, Heilongjiang, and Jehol, the other six provinces are potentially affected by and involved in this incident. 2. Among the six leagues of Inner Mongolia, the Jerim League, the Horchin League, and the Josutu League were reorganized by a powerful neighbor after the September 18th Incident and split into the four Xing'an provinces. The current issue is that the powerful neighbor is further expanding, causing unrest in the Xilingol League, Ulanqab League, and Yekhe Joo League from Chahar and Suiyuan to Gansu and Ningxia.

Based on the first point, the impact of this incident will extend China's external troubles from the Northeast to the Northwest, from the Changbai Mountains to the upper reaches of the Yellow River. Based on the second point, the powerful neighbor created a Northeast puppet organization through the September 18th Incident and used the three leagues of Inner Mongolia within it as a foundation for invading all of Inner Mongolia. The step-by-step progress is clear. If our country does not take appropriate measures to resolve this incident, its extension to the Northwest will be inevitable.

Although the above situation refers to the entire Inner Mongolia issue, it may not be realized in the short term. What is currently an urgent concern for our country is the coercion of Suiyuan and Shanxi provinces. The North China issue in the minds of the powerful neighboring warlords and ronin actually includes the five provinces of Hebei, Shandong, Chahar, Suiyuan, and Shanxi. Because the authorities of Shanxi and Suiyuan were not tempted, their plans suffered a major setback. As a result, they became angry and dispatched a partial force, ordering Li Shou-hsin to join forces with the Mongol Security Forces to bypass Chahar and approach Bangjiang, threatening the Mongol princes and jointly attacking Jining, remotely controlling Datong. This situation is clear when viewing a map. Therefore, this incident has two roles in terms of its initiation and direction. Fundamentally, it is a step towards enticing all of Inner Mongolia. As a side effect, it is used to solve the so-called North China issue.

In the progress of the situation, we hope that the central government and the Suiyuan authorities will recognize the seriousness of the nature of the incident and deal with it decisively. The policies towards Mongolia since June 1933 are purely domestic affairs and still apply to the enlightened Mongolian leagues, while those who have joined forces with the Li Shou-hsin puppet army must be warned. It is rumored that the Suiyuan army has prepared to prevent the westward expansion of the puppet army. It is hoped that the central government will have a comprehensive plan so that the defenders have something to follow. If Suiyuan is not made a continuation of eastern Chahar, and Shanxi and Suiyuan are used as a barrier to the safety of the Northwest, it can be said that there is some hope. Otherwise, with past lessons in mind, how can the spread of disaster be stopped?

The Establishment of a Non-Aggression Pact by Four Near Eastern Countries: An Important Factor in International Affairs 44

Rome: Turkish, Iranian, Iraqi, and Afghan officials have recently established a non-aggression pact. Italian political figures commented that this is an important factor in international affairs and its impact will be very significant. Britain, in its Near East policy, must take this into account. Because after the establishment of this political group, it will unite 35 million people into one force. This move will undoubtedly cause serious problems for the interests of the British Empire. (19th Havas)

The League of Nations Council to Meet Today to Handle the Italo-Ethiopian Dispute; Italy Sends Aloisi as Representative; Britain Unwilling to Advocate Oil Sanctions, Increasing the Weight of the Crisis 45

Geneva: The regular session of the League of Nations Council is scheduled to hold its first meeting at 11:00 AM tomorrow. French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval will arrive here at 10:20 PM today from Clermont-Ferrand in central France. Most other Council member representatives, including British Foreign Secretary Eden, will arrive tomorrow. League of Nations officials are very concerned about the illness of King George V of England and the potential for a cabinet crisis in France, as they believe that Eden and Laval may not be able to stay in Geneva for long according to their original plans. (19th Havas)

Geneva: When the League of Nations Council meets tomorrow, it will only deal with Ethiopia's request to send personnel to investigate Italian aircraft bombing hospitals, undefended cities, and civilians, and the use of poison gas. Ethiopia's request may be passed, but Italy will also request an investigation into the Ethiopian army's use of dumdum bullets, dismemberment of prisoners, and abuse of the Red Cross. Sanctions issues and the implementation of an oil embargo are matters to be considered by the Committee of Eighteen. The general opinion is that the implementation of an oil embargo will depend on Britain's attitude. If Britain is unwilling to initiate it, no one will advocate it. Many people in Geneva believe that Italy is gradually approaching its doom. If an oil embargo is passed and pushed too far, it may create a dangerous situation, which is not politically appropriate. (19th Reuters)

Geneva: According to our correspondent, if there is any misfortune for King George V of England, the current session of the League of Nations Council will have to be postponed for one or two days before it can be held (originally scheduled for the 20th of this month). As for the dispute between the Soviet Union and Uruguay and the Italo-Ethiopian dispute, because British Foreign Secretary Eden and French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval will be staying here for a very short time, they should be dealt with quickly. Regarding the Italo-Ethiopian dispute, since the breakdown of the reconciliation plan proposed by former British Foreign Secretary Hoare and French Prime Minister Laval in December last year, there has been no change in the diplomatic situation. When the Committee of Thirteen of the Council meets in the future, it will only reiterate its willingness to proceed with reconciliation as soon as possible. As for Committee of Eighteen Chairman Vasconcelos, he will also convene the committee to meet, at which time he may appoint a sub-committee to study the possibility of implementing an oil embargo against Italy and to discuss the political, legal, and practical aspects of this issue. The Committee of Eighteen itself will have to wait until February or March to make a decision, because the attitude of the US Congress towards the new Neutrality Act will not be clear until then. (19th Havas)

Paris: Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval took the train to Clermont-Ferrand in central France at 5:00 PM to stay for a short time before going to Geneva to attend the League of Nations Council meeting. Before leaving, the Prime Minister declared to the press, "I will go to Geneva tomorrow to hold consultations with representatives of other countries, including British representative Eden. This conversation should be helpful to the situation, but my stay will be very short."

The Prime Minister did not mention a word about the domestic political situation. (18th Havas)

Rome: For the League of Nations Council meeting on the 20th of this month, the Italian government has sent Aloisi, the director of the Prime Minister's Office, as its representative. According to semi-official observations, the attitude of the countries currently participating in sanctions towards intensifying sanctions has shown a tendency to ease. Aloisi's attendance at the Council meeting is a very important stage for this fact. It is reported that Aloisi's acceptance of this mission was decided after careful consideration by the Italian government. After the Council meeting, Aloisi will once again defend Italy's views on the Italo-Ethiopian dispute and will hold talks with representatives of various countries outside the meeting, hoping to make the sanctions more moderate. This is the method that the Italian government has decided on. In addition, the Italian government recently sent a note to the League of Nations protesting against the "various barbaric acts of Ethiopia," in order to demonstrate that Ethiopia does not have the qualifications of a civilized country. The Italian side hopes that this note will have an effect. (18th Havas)

Rome Issues Statement: Willing to Maintain European Peace; Colony Policy Not Abandoned 46

A spokesman for the Roman government today issued a statement in a particularly accommodating tone, stating that Italy's reason for not withdrawing from the League of Nations is to comply with the principles of collective security and maintain peace in Europe, and it is eager to continue to contribute its cooperation for peace. As for the plan to conquer East Africa, it is an absolutely necessary move, because Italian territories there are often harmed. This is entirely a colonial issue. As long as the security of the territory is consolidated, Italy will devote all its efforts to promoting the European peace plan. It is rumored that the League of Nations will be more lenient towards Italy. This statement coincides with this rumor. (18th National Telegram)

Problem of Soviet-Uruguayan Break in Relations

Geneva: With a French cabinet crisis about to break out and King George V of England in poor health, French Prime Minister Laval and British Foreign Secretary Eden will not stay here for more than two days to participate in the League of Nations Council meeting. At the Council meeting on the 20th, various major political issues will be discussed quickly, such as the complaint filed by the Soviet Union after Uruguay severed relations. According to our interviewer, the League of Nations Secretariat and the countries concerned have been in contact in recent days, so it will not cause major difficulties. The Council will listen to the statements of the representatives of the Soviet Union and Uruguay, and then entrust three member countries to draft a resolution in order to bring it to a swift conclusion. In general, the Council will recognize that it has no right to judge whether the Soviet complaint is appropriate and will advise the Soviet Union and Uruguay to maintain friendly relations in accordance with the spirit of the League of Nations Covenant. (18th Havas)

Geneva: After Uruguay and the Soviet Union severed diplomatic relations, the Soviet government protested to the League of Nations. The next regular meeting of the Council will be discussed at the beginning of next week. At that time, Soviet Foreign Minister Litvinov and Uruguayan representative Dr. Guani will both attend and make statements. It is expected that the Council will appoint a committee of three countries to draft a resolution acceptable to the countries involved. This dispute is expected to be resolved satisfactorily before the Council adjourns. (19th Havas)

Danzig Administrative Report

Warsaw: League of Nations High Commissioner for the Free City of Danzig, Lester, recently submitted a report to the League of Nations, stating that, from his observation, the Danzig Municipal Council is obviously worrying. The Free City's constitution is guaranteed by the League of Nations, but the City Council constantly violates certain provisions of the constitution. An international committee should be established to investigate these unconstitutional facts and find ways to prevent them from happening again. The powers of the High Commissioner should also be expanded. Even the last City Council election was based on unconstitutional actions. The police have no political function and do not maintain public security, so the results are difficult to be fair. (According to the results of the election, the Nazi Party won 43 seats and the opposition party won 29 seats.) In addition, Danzig Nazi Party leader Forster forcibly ordered his armed party members to swear allegiance to German leader Hitler, which is also reprehensible. However, the relationship between Poland and Danzig is generally satisfactory. (18th Havas)

France Brewing Cabinet Crisis: Herriot Decides to Resign Cabinet Position, Daladier Elected Radical Socialist Leader 47

Following the decision of Minister Without Portfolio Herriot to resign, the Laval cabinet's position has already been affected, and a major cabinet crisis is expected to erupt in the middle of next week. Herriot met with Prime Minister Laval this afternoon, saying that he would formally resign after the Prime Minister returned from Geneva, likely on Tuesday. Meanwhile, the Executive Committee of the Radical Socialist Party is scheduled to meet tomorrow. If the committee decides that all cabinet members affiliated with the party should also resign, then those cabinet members will retire at the same time as Herriot, also likely next week. The cabinet members met today, with Herriot attending, and reaffirmed their decision to resign from their cabinet positions and not to nominate a candidate for party leader. People here are calm about the political situation, but there is intense criticism of Herriot's decision, with some harsh rebukes, echoing the tone of the right-wing parties. These parties, who support the current cabinet, all say that if a cabinet crisis breaks out, the financial sector will inevitably panic. Regarding this, the Governor of the Bank of France, Tannery, warned Herriot. However, the stock market situation remains stable as usual. (Havas dispatch on the 18th)

Paris: The position of leader of the Radical Socialist Party has been vacant since Minister Without Portfolio Herriot resigned in December last year. The party's Executive Committee held an election at 3:00 PM today, and left-wing leader and former Prime Minister Daladier was elected amidst cheers. Daladier is strongly opposed to the Laval cabinet. (Havas dispatch on the 19th)

South Tyrol Province: Becoming a Large Military Camp, Italians Internally Oppose War Against Abyssinia, New Recruits Fear Distant Expedition and Lack Martial Spirit 48

Innsbruck: Contrary to widespread rumors of serious unrest in South Tyrol province, which the authorities strongly deny, a special correspondent from Reuters today visited the area to investigate. After crossing the Brenner Pass border with barbed wire obstacles, they noticed secret police following them. Italy has transformed South Tyrol province into a large military camp, with at least 20,000 troops stationed there. The machine gun teams stationed on the mountains were practicing with straw figures of Abyssinians when the correspondent arrived. Every Tyrolean encountered opposes the Italian war. The Italian authorities seem capable of handling the current situation without doubt, but the morale of the troops is even more important. South Tyrol province is now feeling the impact of sanctions. It is reported that some new recruits cried upon hearing that they were being transferred to Africa. The soldiers lack martial spirit, and their daily allowance is less than two shillings. The correspondent learned that about 1,400 people have fled Tyrol into Austria and Bavaria. (Reuters dispatch on the 19th)

Italian Military Victory Reported, Abyssinia Denies 49

Addis Ababa: Italian sources report a major victory for the Italian army on the southern front in the Doria River region, killing 4,000 Abyssinian soldiers and advancing 120 kilometers. A communique issued here denies this, stating, "The above news was released by the Italian side, apparently to influence the shape of the upcoming meetings of the League of Nations Council and the committees dealing with the Italo-Abyssinian dispute. According to information from the southern front, the Abyssinian army believes it is necessary to change its position to avoid Italian air raids." The communique also denies the Italian claim in its note to the League of Nations that Abyssinian troops misused the Red Cross flag. (Havas dispatch on the 18th)

Abyssinian Troop Movements: Preparing for Counterattack 50

Addis Ababa: Recent troop movements of the Abyssinian army on the front lines suggest an intention to clear open ground in front of the Italian lines, to facilitate a counterattack in the future. According to this agency's reporter, current front-line military operations are of the most serious nature, unprecedented since the start of the war. (Havas dispatch on the 18th)

Italy Responds to Sweden: Friendly Tone 51

Stockholm, Sweden: Swedish Foreign Minister Sandler stated in parliament today, regarding the recent destruction of the Swedish Red Cross relief team by Italian planes in Abyssinia, that a weakening Italy would not benefit all of Europe. While the outrage against the atrocities is justified, this should not lead Sweden to adopt overly severe sanctions. At the same time, the Italian government has responded to Sweden's protest against the Italian air raid, resolutely rejecting the claim of intentionally harming the Swedish relief team. The Italian response was delivered to the Swedish ambassador in Rome and is said to be friendly and clear. (Reuters dispatch on the 18th)

20-30 U.S. Munitions Factories: Violating Neutrality Act, Hull Refers to Justice Department 52

Washington: Secretary of State Hull announced today that he has submitted the names of 20-30 munitions factories that have failed to register with the State Department in compliance with the Neutrality Act to Attorney General Cummings. (Reuters dispatch on the 18th)

U.S. Bonus Amendment: Defeated in Senate 53

Washington: The Thomas Amendment to the veterans' bonus bill, which advocated paying bonuses through inflation (i.e., printing more money), was defeated in the Senate today by a vote of 64 to 27. No decision has been made on the original bill, and the Senate has adjourned until Monday. (National Telegraph dispatch on the 18th)

British King's Condition Not Improving: Cardiologist Leaving Palace Raises Speculation, People Anxious, Prayers Held in Churches Nationwide 54

The latest bulletin reporting on the King's condition is quite serious in nature, causing increasing anxiety throughout the British Empire. Prayers were held in churches nationwide over the past two days. According to official sources from Sandringham this morning, the King's sleep was restless, but his strength remained. A bulletin will be issued tonight. The Archbishop of Canterbury said in the cathedral that the King's strength was still good, and that the royal doctors were skilled, so there was hope for recovery. The renowned cardiologist, Sir Maurice Cassidy, who was consulted by the three royal physicians, left Sandringham yesterday afternoon, raising speculation. The King's two granddaughters also returned to London yesterday. The King's daughter, who came to Sandringham yesterday, inquired in detail about her father's condition from her mother and siblings after entering the palace. The King's third son, the Duke of Gloucester, was unable to attend to his bedside due to a sore throat, but it is said that his throat pain is now gradually improving. The King's two nurses are constantly at his side. Since dawn today, many people have gathered in front of Buckingham Palace to inquire about the King's condition, showing the nation's deep concern. Despite the cold, men, women, and children are waiting in groups for the release of bulletins. Hundreds of news reporters from around the world have gathered in the town of Dowsinhham to gather news nearby. The lights in the King's bedroom remained on all night, and the nurses quietly moved about, watching the King's movements. The lights were only turned off after dawn. (Reuters dispatch on the 19th)

King George V, currently suffering from tracheobronchitis, is convalescing at Sandringham House. According to a bulletin issued by the royal physicians at 10:00 PM tonight, his condition has not changed. This shows that since the afternoon bulletin, the King's condition has neither worsened nor improved. A subsequent midnight bulletin stated: "His Majesty is now resting peacefully." The citizens of London were shocked upon hearing the news of the King's illness. This afternoon, people from all walks of life gathered in front of Buckingham Palace, waiting to see the bulletins released by the attending physicians. When the evening newspapers were published, people on the streets rushed to buy them, eager to be the first to see the news. The people's anxiety is evident. It is rumored that the granddaughters of the King, Princess Elizabeth and Princess Margaret (daughters of the King's second son, the Duke of York, who have been at the palace since Christmas), have returned to London from Sandringham House, adding to the uneasiness. The Archbishop of Canterbury led a sincere prayer this afternoon at Canterbury Cathedral. Other Catholic churches in the southern diocese were also ordered to hold prayers, wishing the King a speedy recovery. This is another reason for the people's anxiety. Prime Minister Baldwin, who had intended to go to Chequers for the weekend, has canceled his trip due to the King's illness. It is learned that the royal physicians, Lord Dawson, Sir William Shearer, and Sir Hugh Whitwell, are all attending to his bedside. Sir Hugh Whitwell has been a royal physician for over 20 years. The renowned cardiologist, Sir Maurice Cassidy, is still at Sandringham House after being summoned from Harley Street this morning. (Havas dispatch on the 18th)

Prime Minister Baldwin has canceled his customary weekend outing to remain on Downing Street. It is understood that this move is due to the dangerous condition of King George. Meanwhile, Home Secretary Simon receives hourly reports on the condition, as it is the Home Secretary's duty to personally announce the King's death. (National Telegraph dispatch on the 18th)

The bulletin from Sandringham Palace at 3:30 PM today stated that King George had a few hours of peaceful sleep, but his heart was very weak and his pulse was even weaker. Princess Elizabeth and Princess Rose have returned to the palace from London. The King's secretary, Sir William, has also arrived here. The general public attaches great importance to their arrival. However, Home Secretary Simon is still at his private residence. It is understood that the government may organize a Council of State to govern during the King's illness. Meanwhile, the King's Lynn Hospital, ten miles from Sandringham Palace, has prepared a large supply of oxygen in case of emergency. (National Telegraph dispatch on the 18th)

The Prince of Wales and the Duke of York, sons of the King, arrived at Sandringham House in England this morning by car, traveling from London. They will return here tonight. It is generally believed that the Prince of Wales will meet with Prime Minister Baldwin. (Havas dispatch on the 19th)

England, Newham: This agency's special correspondent reports that this town, which is a stone's throw from Sandringham House, has become a gathering place for news hunters since news of King's illness broke out. The situation today is noteworthy. More than 50 journalists and photographers arrived here early in the morning. All the hotels are crowded. In addition to providing proper hospitality, the proprietors are well aware that these uninvited guests may not go to bed at night and will be sitting up all night waiting for news from Sandringham House, so they have specially set up tables and chairs for them to write. However, the palace gates are heavily guarded, and reporters are not allowed to enter. They all stand in front of the palace gate, illuminated by the palace lights, imagining the tense situation inside. Seeing the King's flag flying in the wind on the roof, one can imagine that the King is safe. It was learned this afternoon that cardiologist Sir Maurice Cassidy has left the palace and does not intend to return, which caused a great shock. People speculated that perhaps Sir Maurice Cassidy was also powerless. However, palace officials said that Sir Maurice's departure should not be taken too seriously. (Havas dispatch on the 18th)

Czechoslovakia Strengthening Military: Defending National Territory with All Efforts, President Concurrently Serves as Army Grand Marshal 55

Prague, Czechoslovakia: President Benes, in his capacity as president, has assumed the position of Army Grand Marshal and issued a proclamation to the army, stating, "We have no expectations of other countries' territory, but we are determined to defend all of our national territory with all our efforts, and no sacrifice will be spared." Chaco Peace Treaty: Officially Signed Today, Contains Four Items 56

Buenos Aires, Argentina: The Chaco dispute peace treaty has been accepted by both the Bolivian and Paraguayan governments. The peace conference is scheduled to hold a public meeting tomorrow to officially sign the treaty. The representatives of the arbitrating countries, namely Argentina, Brazil, Chile, Uruguay, and the United States, have already signed the draft. The contents of this treaty are divided into four items:

* Restoration of diplomatic relations between the belligerent countries

* Exchange of prisoners of war between the belligerent countries

* Compensation for war damages

* Guarantees for the future. (Havas dispatch on the 19th)

Trip to Nanchang (Part Two): Inauguration of the Yunan Section of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway and Other Matters 57

Grand Inauguration Ceremony: On January 15th, at approximately 7:00 AM, the inauguration ceremony reception office notified guests at various hotels that vehicles were prepared to transport them to Nanchang Station to attend the ceremony. At 9:00 AM, guests successively boarded buses to the assembly area in front of the station. This was a shed made of reeds, large enough to accommodate a thousand people, decorated with lanterns and colorful ribbons. On the stage, in addition to the national flag and the portrait of Dr. Sun Yat-sen, there was a loudspeaker for the speakers to amplify their voices. A horizontal banner read "Yunan Section Inauguration Ceremony". On both sides were long couplets that read, "Six hundred *li* of winding tracks, travelers rejoice, celebrating the connection between Zhejiang and Jiangxi provinces," and "Hundreds of people united with sincerity, the project completed successfully, working together to serve the nation." More than six hundred people attended, including the Director-General of the railway, Zeng Yangfu; the Chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, Huang Shaohong; the Chairman of the Jiangxi Provincial Government, Xiong Shihui; representatives from industry, banking, and the press; and guests from Beijing, Shanghai, Hangzhou, and other places. Director-General Zeng Yangfu presided over the meeting and delivered a report. Following this, the Director and Chief Engineer of the Railway Bureau, Du Zhenyuan, and the Deputy Director and Deputy Chief Engineer, Hou Jiashen, reported on the construction process. Because more than two thousand people died during the construction of this section of the railway – some killed by bandits, some drowned, and some succumbed to epidemics – Zeng Yangfu asked the guests in attendance to stand in silence for five minutes to mourn the deceased workers. Subsequently, Huang Shaohong, Xiong Shihui, representatives from the Provincial Party Headquarters, the German Embassy's Representative, Fischer, and representatives from the Sinot-Wahalf Company delivered speeches. The representative of the banking group, Cui Baoshu, also read speeches written by T.V. Soong and Song Hanzhang. Afterwards, ushers guided the attendees out of the assembly area for a photograph in front of the station. Then everyone boarded the special train from Hangzhou to Nanchang. At 12:20 PM, the train departed for Liangjiadu to hold the groundbreaking ceremony for the Nanping section.

Groundbreaking Ceremony for the Nanping Section: According to the Railway Bureau's survey, the Nanping section will begin at a place called Hexi on a tributary of the Fu River and end at Pingxiang, with a length of 263 kilometers. This is more than 20 kilometers shorter than the northern route. The terrain along the route is also relatively flat, and it can also avoid the need to spend large sums of money to rebuild the bridge over the Fu River tributary. Therefore, it was decided to adopt the southern route. Around 1:00 PM on January 15th, the groundbreaking ceremony was held near the western abutment of the large Shu Fu River Bridge at Liangjiadu. The Railway Bureau set up an altar on a yellow earth mound. After the special train stopped at the site, Zeng Yangfu, Xiong Shihui, Huang Shaohong, and guests from all walks of life disembarked and walked there. After firecrackers were set off and the meeting commenced, Zeng Yangfu gave a brief report, expressing hope that they would continue the past spirit from the groundbreaking day and hold a grand inauguration ceremony for the Nanping section one and a half years later. Then, together with Xiong Shihui, Huang Shaohong, and Chinese and foreign guests, everyone picked up duck-bill hoes and shovels wrapped with red cloth and ribbons and performed the groundbreaking. In this way, over a hundred railway workers began construction.

Visit to the Fu River Bridge: The Fu River Bridge is the largest bridge on the entire Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway line, with fourteen spans, a width of 35 *chi*, and a total length of 490 meters. It features steel plate girders, concrete piers, wooden piles, and concrete foundations, costing over 730,000 yuan. It is a bridge for both railway and highway use. The railway is located in the middle, for trains to pass, and triangular cantilever structures are extended on both sides (not yet completed) for cars to pass. At this time, the north wind was strong, but everyone walked across the bridge with great interest. Afterwards, the special train crossed the bridge again to pick up the guests and return to Nanchang. According to Zeng Yangfu, "If a highway bridge had to be built over the Fu River, it would have required 600,000 yuan. Now, by cantilevering off the railway bridge, it only cost 200,000 yuan, saving 400,000 yuan."

Lizhishi Banquet: The special train left Liangjiadu at 1:30 PM and returned to Nanchang. At 3:30 PM, it arrived at Nanchang Station. The guests then took public buses to the Lizhishi to attend the banquet hosted by the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Company. The Lizhishi is Nanchang's military club, built on a high ground by the Gan River. The building is I-shaped, palace-style, and three-stories, with one story underground. The auditorium can be used for speeches, plays, sports, banquets, and movies. There are commandments handwritten by Chiang Kai-shek. Although the decor cannot be said to be luxurious, it can be described as very clean and beautiful. Seats were arranged in the auditorium, in five vertical rows, accommodating over six hundred people. It is said that this was Nanchang's largest banquet in terms of the number of people. At 5:30 PM, Zeng Yangfu invited Chairman Xiong and Huang to take their seats, while he himself sat in the presiding seat. Western food was served, consisting of only one soup, one dish, and one dessert, but these six hundred-plus servings required knives, forks, and plates that reportedly had to be specially borrowed from Jiujiang. During the banquet, Zeng Yangfu rose to speak, thanking the guests for their presence and wishing them a pleasant journey. He also said, "Chairman Xiong has four major railway policies: the Zhejiang-Jiangxi, Jiangxi-Fujian, Jiangxi-Guangdong, and Jiangxi-Anhui lines. Now, the inauguration ceremony for the Yunan section is being held, with more than six hundred guests. We hope that when the Nanping section opens next year, there will be twelve hundred guests, and we hope that Chairman Xiong will build an even larger dining hall than this one for us to feast the guests. Furthermore, we hope that when the Jiangxi-Guangdong section opens in the future, there will be forty-eight hundred guests; when the Jiangxi-Fujian section opens, there will be nine thousand guests; and when the Jiangxi-Anhui section opens, there will be tens of thousands of guests." This made everyone smile. Less than a minute after Zeng finished sitting, he suddenly rose again to speak, "For the completion of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway, we must also thank one person, and that is the Chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, Huang Shaohong. Everyone should raise a glass to him." Zeng's social skills can be seen from these instances. The banquet did not end until 7:00 PM.

Xiong Shihui's Progress: After the dinner, more than twenty reporters from Beijing, Shanghai, Hangzhou, and Western newspapers jointly interviewed Xiong Shihui. Commissioner Xiao led them into the reception room, where they sat around in a circle, leaving a chair in the middle for Xiong to sit and talk. Ten minutes later, Xiong entered the room, wearing a yellow Zhongshan suit made of straight-woven silk. His hair was neatly combed, and he looked healthy. Considering he was almost forty years old, he still looked like a young soldier. However, judging from his words and actions, the arduous political life he had been living in Jiangxi in recent years had cultivated a restraint in his demeanor compared to his Shanghai days. He had the earnest and practical demeanor of a statesman. He answered almost all of the reporters' questions earnestly and specifically. He said, "Although the main force of the Red Army has left Jiangxi, small groups of bandits in remote areas of Jiangxi have not been completely eliminated, but they are absolutely not a cause for concern and will absolutely not return to Jiangxi. The construction of highways reached more than ten thousand kilometers last year, and construction is still actively underway this year. The earthwork and the transport of wood and stone are all done by the people, and the government is only paving the prepared materials." He also said, "Most of the land deeds and grain coupons in the Red areas have indeed been destroyed by the Communists, but now they are being reorganized using the Baojia system, which is even more perfect than the old system. This is because the Red Army did not flatten the field boundaries. Since most of Jiangxi is mountainous, leveling the field boundaries would prevent the fields in the mountainous areas from storing water. Moreover, if they were to carry out this work, the effort they would expend would be more troublesome than our construction of highways. Regarding Zhejiang, after the completion of the Yunan section of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway, my intention is to give priority to supplying Zhejiang with the special products of our province, such as rice and grain, because Zhejiang still has to buy foreign rice. Agricultural cooperatives are now progressing smoothly. For example, the tangerines of Nanfeng are very famous. In the past, even Nanchang rarely saw them. Now, on the one hand, we are teaching them how to improve cultivation, and on the other hand, we are finding ways to transport and sell them. Now, not only does Nanchang have Nanfeng tangerines, but Shanghai also has them." He also said, "When President Chiang was stationed in Nanchang earlier this year, he was extremely concerned about the political construction and revitalization work in Jiangxi. Although he has now gone to Nanjing to preside over the central government affairs, he is unable to revisit Jiangxi, but his concern for the political situation in the province is as it was in the past and has not been forgotten. As for the thinking of the people in the province, before the bandits were eliminated, most of them held a passive attitude, but now they are all trending towards a more active one, so they are able to assist the government's political work with all their strength. For example, the construction of major highways and the completion of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway are mostly due to the power of the people. What Director Zeng said just now, that I have four major railway policies, refers to the Jiangxi-Guangdong, Jiangxi-Fujian, Jiangxi-Zhejiang, and Jiangxi-Anhui trunk lines. Because I had previously advocated that merely completing the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway would not fully serve the main trunk line south of the Yangtze River, I proposed the addition of the other three lines to extend to the southern provinces and become the center of the southeastern railway network. This plan is now being worked on in cooperation with all parties concerned." While Xiong was speaking, colleagues from Nanchang held a tea party at the Lizhishi, chatting happily during the gathering. Everyone only dispersed after 9:00 PM.

Provincial Government Tea Party: According to the original schedule, guests were supposed to leave Nanchang on the night of the 15th after dinner at the Lizhishi. Later, because the Jiangxi Provincial Government scheduled a tea party for guests from all walks of life at the Provincial Government at 3:00 PM on the 16th, they stayed in Nanchang for another day. During these twenty-four hours, on the one hand, they could take the opportunity to sightsee in Nanchang City and nearby scenic spots, and on the other hand, they could also investigate several of the more important undertakings in Jiangxi and several of the works that the Provincial Government has been striving for recently. At 3:00 PM on the afternoon of the 16th, more than two hundred guests from all walks of life gathered in the grand auditorium of the Jiangxi Provincial Government for a grand tea party. Chairman Xiong and all the members of the Provincial Government personally served with diligence. First, attendants distributed a glass of "Cognac" wine to each guest, who drank and chatted at the same time. Tea and Western-style desserts were also prepared for guests to take at will, with freedom of movement and no restrictions. Although the format was simple, the meaning was very rich. It lasted for over an hour before dispersing. When dispersing, more than ten volumes of "Jiangxi Undertakings Series" and various outlines of the recent work of the Provincial Government were also distributed. After the tea party, guests rushed back to their hotels to pack their luggage. Before 5:00 PM, they gathered at Nanchang Station to board the train. Xiong Guangdu and all the members of the Provincial Committee and the heads of various agencies were also at the station to see them off. At 5:15 PM, our special train said goodbye to Nanchang amidst the melodious sound of military music. At 6:00 PM on the afternoon of the 17th, we arrived at the bank of the river. The special train returned to Shanghai that night.

Actively Revitalizing the Countryside: Jiangxi is entirely an agricultural province. After being severely damaged by the Red Bandits in the past few years, the bankruptcy of the countryside has reached an unimaginable state. Now, although they have been suppressed, the revitalization work can be considered the most difficult and arduous. After recovering the bandit areas, the Jiangxi Provincial Government devoted all its energy to this arduous revitalization work. In the past year, it has made considerable progress. The organization and work overview of their revitalization of the countryside is roughly as follows. Under the goal of revitalizing the countryside, the Provincial Rural Cooperative Committee, the Agricultural Institute, and the Jiangxi Rural Service Guidance Office of the National Economic Council have been established. The main work of the Rural Cooperative Committee is divided into three major categories: rural cooperation, such as cooperative education, cooperative administration, cooperative loans, and assistance in supply and transportation; rural economy, such as disaster relief for bandit-stricken rural areas and drought relief for rural areas; and rural land management. There is a total of 2 million yuan in funding, which is used exclusively for loans and various relief efforts. The main work of the Agricultural Institute includes the establishment of five departments: plant production, animal production, promotion, agricultural economics, and general affairs. It engages in the development of production and promotion. The start-up cost is 300,000 yuan, and the annual cost is 200,000 yuan. The Jiangxi Rural Service Guidance Office of the National Economic Council has established eight experimental areas throughout Jiangxi Province. Its main tasks are rural education, sanitation, cooperative guidance, livestock improvement, and disease prevention.

Page 11

According to news from the Provincial Government, this year's focus on rural revitalization work is on water conservancy, with water conservancy as the center of construction. The Provincial Water Conservancy Office has divided the entire province into eight major engineering offices, engaging in the following tasks: dike construction, tree planting, canal excavation, and river dredging. The method of conscription is implemented, that is, people perform labor service. Each able-bodied man performs labor service for a maximum of twenty days and a minimum of five days. The method of distribution is proportional to the amount of engineering work in a certain place and the number of able-bodied men. Also, the original population of Jiangxi Province was 24 million, but since the Red Bandits disrupted it, there are now only about 17 million.

Handling Rural Land

The rural land of Jiangxi Province has been repeatedly divided and surveyed by the Red Bandits, resulting in changes in boundaries, loss of deeds, and complicated and chaotic ownership and tenancy relationships, making disputes prone to occur. This has a huge impact on the stability of rural order and the recovery of unemployment. After Chairman Chiang promulgated the Regulations on the Handling of Rural Land in Various Provinces within the Bandit Suppression Area by the General Headquarters of the Three Provinces in the 21st year of the Republic, he redeployed to Nanchang and reiterated the previous order, actively implementing it. He also considered that rural affairs in the recovered areas were numerous and personnel were few, making it difficult to establish rural revitalization committees at all levels. Therefore, he used the articles of association of the Cooperative Preparatory Society to stipulate that each preparatory society should act as a rural committee in a township or town, so as to universally handle land ownership registration and other work. In January of last year, the headquarters also held a land handling training course to train land handling staff. In February, it ordered the Rural Cooperative Committee to direct these personnel to preside over the land handling affairs in the recovered counties and districts. Later, because it coincided with the spring plowing season, it based on the actual situation, using the shortest time, the least manpower, and the greatest efficiency as the criterion for carrying out this work. The handling situation is as follows: Maintenance after spring plowing and autumn harvest: After receiving orders in February last year, the Rural Cooperative Association selected cadres from the members of the headquarters' land training class to serve as land handling instructors, dividing them into fourteen counties and districts such as Lianhua, Yongxin, and Xiushui, where bandit disasters were more serious and land was more chaotic, to start work. It also guided and utilized the Cooperative Preparatory Society to properly mediate disputes between landowners and tenants, so as to ensure that spring plowing would not be delayed and autumn harvest would not cause disputes. It has resolved more than 200 land disputes. For fields that were abandoned due to tenancy disputes, after guidance and urging to increase reclamation, there were more than 18,000 *mu*. After the autumn harvest, it prevented landlords from forcing rent collection in 18 cases. It has indeed achieved considerable results in stabilizing the order of the recovered countryside. Handling land registration: In addition to guiding and utilizing the Cooperative Preparatory Society to mediate disputes between landowners and tenants, the land handling instructors in each county actively promoted the establishment of rural revitalization committees in each county and district to handle land registration work. According to reports from the heads of various county bureaus, 9 counties and districts, including Pingxiang and Shuhua, have established rural revitalization committees. Among them, Lianhua County alone registered more than 110,000 *mu* of land. Other county bureaus are still in progress. However, since September of last year, because the predetermined period expired and funding was unavailable, the Rural Cooperative Association has withdrawn these instructors. This handling work has been transferred to each county and district for separate supervision and continued handling.

Effectiveness of Special Education

Jiangxi Province has suffered from bandit disasters for many years, with almost four-fifths of the province falling into bandit areas. Wherever the Red Bandits passed, the local area was ravaged, the people were brutally killed, the social economy collapsed, and rural enterprises were destroyed. The severity of the damage is unprecedented. However, this is only the tangible bandit disaster, and the ideological poisoning suffered by the general public is truly frightening. The Red Bandits established Lenin Primary Schools, Public Clubs, and other reactionary educational institutions in the areas they occupied. Each county had hundreds of them, doing everything they could to numb and entice the people. As a result, the adults and children in the bandit areas exhibited abnormal and immoral consciousness and behavior. If measures are not taken to correct and remedy this, the consequences will be unimaginable. Chairman Chiang, seeing this, instructed the Jiangxi Provincial Government to establish schools as soon as the bandit areas were gradually recovered, so that children would have books to read and adults and able-bodied men would have the opportunity to make up for their education. All measures should not be bound by conventions and should be tailored to the specific circumstances to achieve the goal of subtle influence. The Provincial Government followed this instruction and, with reference to the Interim Measures for the Implementation of Social Education in Special Areas promulgated and implemented by the Central Standing Committee, implemented it in the recovered bandit areas to remedy the basic education of adults and children who had been communized, called Special Education. The Department of Education stipulated plans and started implementation, hoping to use the method of combining management, education, nurturing, and hygiene to provide the people in the recovered bandit areas with transformative, civic, vocational, and self-defense training to correct their thinking, build their character, develop their livelihoods, and support their survival, so as to achieve the ultimate goal of national revival. Special education is aimed at rescuing the bandit areas after their recovery, with education as the center, focusing on correcting the erroneous thinking of the people, training local self-defense, and increasing rural production. It aims to train the people and children to thoroughly understand the crimes of the Red Bandits and the fallacies of their arguments, so as to firmly believe in the Three Principles of the People and love the country; to train the people and children to have civic qualifications, self-defense capabilities, and productive skills, so as to achieve social peace and people's happy lives; to establish the foundation of education in the recovered bandit areas, and strive to promote it as a goal. The Provincial Government believes that the talents who implement special education must have special training. Therefore, in February of last year, it recruited two classes for the first training course, totaling 84 people. After four months of rigorous training, 80 people graduated. In June, it recruited a second term and expanded the training of special education teachers in the recovered counties in order to adapt to the needs of each county. It specially established two summer training classes and a research class to cultivate special education guidance talents in the recovered counties and seek the progress of special education. As a result of the recruitment, there were 84 people in the summer class, 91 people in the second training class, and 38 people in the research class. Afterwards, the training periods expired one after another. After passing the examinations, 83 people graduated from the former and 91 people graduated from the latter, and all have been assigned to serve in the recovered counties. In total, 254 students have graduated from various terms, and 38 students are still in school. Since the implementation of special education, it has achieved considerable results. If we continue to work hard and promote it continuously, in a few years, the people of the entire province will have self-reliant skills and sound character.

Decline of the Porcelain and Sugar Industries

The porcelain of Jingdezhen in Jiangxi has a long history of thousands of years. It is not only a specialty of Jiangxi, but also a precious product of China. During the Ming and Qing dynasties, it was at its peak. During the Qing dynasty, the Jingdezhen Imperial Porcelain Factory was renamed the Imperial Kiln Factory. During the Qianlong period, Tang Ying, an official of the Ministry of Internal Affairs, was appointed to supervise the Imperial Kiln Factory, bringing together skilled workers and concentrating on craftsmanship. The style was modeled on the simple and rustic style of ancient porcelain, and the colorful and gorgeous style of Western enamel. Other techniques such as porcelain plate photography and lifelike painting were also used. At that time, the factories competed with each other, constantly innovating. Therefore, it enjoyed a reputation throughout the world, and sales were extremely brisk. Unfortunately, after its peak, Jingdezhen suffered many military disasters, resulting in huge losses. By the time of the opening of the five ports, foreign porcelain poured in again, and the porcelain industry of Jingdezhen declined sharply. Since the Republic of China, no special management has been set up for porcelain administration, and it has been allowed to grow and die on its own. After 1919, it was repeatedly ravaged by the Red Bandits, and its decline deepened. In its heyday, there were hundreds of kilns and hundreds of thousands of workers. Porcelain exports reached countries in Europe and the United States, and the total annual turnover was often around 20 million yuan. According to a recent survey by people in the porcelain industry, in the past two years, the total annual value of porcelain exports was less than four to five million yuan, and the amount of porcelain exported overseas has dropped to fifty to sixty thousand *dan*. The extent of its decline is truly heartbreaking. The provincial authorities have long had plans for improvement, but they have been hampered by financial difficulties. It is now known that the Provincial Government has established the Jiangxi Pottery Administration Bureau in Jingdezhen in order to promote the development of the porcelain industry, so as to carry out rectification and improvement. Chinese sugar production used to occupy an important position in the world. Jiangxi's sugar industry also ranks third in the country. In its peak years, annual production exceeded 300,000 *dan*, not only being self-sufficient, but also having a surplus for sale outside the province. In recent years, production has decreased daily and sales have stagnated. Those who used to supply other provinces are now relying on others. The degree of degradation is shocking, and the loss of resources is great. Now that the Red Bandits have been suppressed, efforts are being made to revive various industries. Therefore, plans are being made to restore this sugar industry, which once had a good reputation. It is now known that the Provincial Government has resolved to send personnel to carry and prepare forms, and to conduct field investigations in various sugar-producing areas. After the survey is obtained and the customs report is received, a systematic statistics and research will be made on the various situations of sugar cane planting and sugar production in the province and the dumping of foreign sugar. The Provincial government will also conduct a systematic statistical study and research, and will realistically rectify the areas where sugarcane planting and sugar production in this province should be improved and supported.

Nanchang News Industry: In recent years, the news industry in Nanchang has made considerable progress due to the government's and people's recognition of the great relationship between the news industry and the country, society, politics, economy, and culture, and their vigorous support and promotion, as well as the efforts of colleagues to seek progress and struggle. Whether in terms of speech, editing, or business, it has progressed more than before. According to the reporter's investigation, the general situation is as follows: News agencies include the Central News Agency branch, the Jiangxi News Agency sponsored by the Provincial Party Headquarters, and the private Kuanglu News Agency and Jiangxi News Agency; Newspapers include the Republican Daily sponsored by the Provincial Party Headquarters, which publishes three major sheets every day, with a daily circulation of about 2,500 copies, and monthly advertising revenue of about 600 yuan; the Xinwen Bao, which publishes two and a half sheets every day (the Provincial Government subsidizes a portion of the funds each month), with a daily circulation of over 1,000 copies, and monthly advertising revenue of 400 to 500 yuan; the Min Bao, which publishes two and a half sheets every day, with monthly advertising revenue of over 600 yuan, and a daily circulation of about 1,000 copies; the Gongshang Bao, which publishes two and a half sheets every day, with a smaller circulation, and monthly advertising revenue of 400 to 500 yuan; and the Shang Bao, which publishes two and a half sheets every day, with a smaller circulation and monthly advertising revenue of 200 to 300 yuan. In addition, there are evening newspapers (half sheet) and small newspapers, with a daily circulation of several hundred copies, but the advertising revenue is unknown. Other larger counties have small stone-printed newspapers, but most of them are run by the Party Headquarters. Also, in order to avoid difficulties in work and unify the records, the reporters of various newspapers in Nanchang organized a reporters' interview team in December of last year. According to this kind of organization, it may hinder the progress of the newspaper, but in a special environment, it only serves as a transitional measure, and it seems harmless. (Huating)

Activities of the Mongolian Security Forces in Western Suiyuan: Zhuo Shihai's Troops Display Unusual Movements, Telegraphing Li Shou-hsin's Puppet Troops Arriving at Daqingmen, Kang Wang Passing Through Suiyuan to Jin to Report on Anti-Communism 58

Min Security Regiment Commander Zhan Fangzhen Detained 59

—Zhan Was Originally a Notorious Bandit in Southern Fujian—Xiamen Dispatch: Zhan Fangzhen, the commander of the 7th Security Regiment, was originally a notorious bandit in southern Fujian, rampaging in the Anxi, Hua'an, and Zhangping counties for over a decade. Last year, he was persuaded by Suiyuan and incorporated into the provincial government forces. Wu Zhuzhong, the commander of the 2nd Battalion of his regiment, was from Zhan's original bandit forces. Ye Chengqing, the commander of the 1st Battalion, and Wang Zizhiwang, the commander of the 3rd Battalion, were transferred from other local militias after incorporation and integration. On the morning of the 16th, Zhan traveled from Zhangzhou to Zhangpu in his private car with the Security Department inspection committee members Jiang Lei and Hu Jiwu. They stayed at the Weisheng Lou Hotel. At 7 p.m., he was summoned by Chen Qi, the commander of the 80th Division, and went to the division headquarters to meet Chen. Chen immediately ordered Zhan's detention. The 7th Regiment's office in Zhangzhou was also searched, one of Zhan's guards was arrested, and Zhan's private car was impounded. To prevent leaks, long-distance telephone lines from Zhangzhou to Zhangpu and Punan were cut off that night. At the same time, a secret telegram was sent to the 80th Division troops stationed in Zhangpu to disarm the 1st, 2nd, and 3rd Battalions of Zhan's regiment during roll call at 7 a.m. on the 17th. Subsequently, Wang, the brigade commander of the 80th Division's 239th Brigade, and Chen, the brigade commander of the Independent 39th Brigade, arrived in Zhangpu from Zhangzhou. After addressing the officers and soldiers of the 1st Battalion under Ye Chengqing and the 2nd Battalion under Wang Zhigang, the firearms were returned to them. Furthermore, the 80th Division headquarters ordered the troops stationed in Punan on the evening of the 16th to detain Zhan's family members residing in Punan. During the arrest, Zhan's family guards resisted, resulting in one death and one serious injury. Zhan's wife, concubines, children, and nephews, four people were arrested. The 80th Fujian Division's detention of Zhan was carried out based on a secret telegram from the Security Department. The operation was extremely secretive and swift. Zhangzhou, Zhangpu, and Punan took simultaneous action to resolve the situation overnight. The reasons for Zhan's detention are still unknown. However, it is undeniable that Zhan was originally a notorious bandit in southern Fujian with poor discipline. There must be a reason for resolving the situation. (January 18th)

The 80th Division Stationed in Zhangzhou Resolves the Zhangzhou Secret Service Team: The Team Is Accused of Indiscipline 60

Thirty-Nine Killed During Disarmament Xiamen Dispatch The Special Service First Team of the Investigation Department of the Zhangzhou Garrison Headquarters, led by Zheng Yuanlong, the deputy team leader Wu Jinlai, the Second Team led by Hong Haojie, and the Third Team leader Zhang Yuting were formed by integrating local bandits from Zhangzhou and affiliated with the Investigation Department of the Garrison Headquarters as a special service team, stationed in the southeast suburbs of the city. However, even after being incorporated, they continued to be undisciplined, extorting the villagers in the four suburban areas and privately collecting donations. The people repeatedly presented complaints to Chen Qi, the commander of the 80th Division and the Zhangzhou Garrison Commander. Commander Chen summoned Zheng, Hong, Zhang, and others several times, sternly warning them to mend their ways. However, they ultimately did not change. In recent months, the accumulated complaints piled up. On the 14th, Commander Chen dispatched personnel to the southeastern villages to summon the three team leaders and all the troops into the city, ostensibly for roll call and verification of firearms. The three teams did not suspect anything. At 10 a.m. on the 15th, First Team Leader Zheng Yuanlong led 28 men, Second Team Leader Hong Haojie led 28 men, and Third Team Leader Zhang Yuting led 24 men into the city one after another, gathering at Zhongshan Park. Prior to this, all soldiers of the 478th Regiment under the 80th Division, led by Du Kan, were fully armed and guarded inside and outside Zhongshan Park. At 11 a.m., the three teams gathered in front of the memorial platform in Zhongshan Park to listen to the roll call. The special service team was in the front row, followed by hundreds of soldiers from the 80th Division's 478th Regiment. Soldiers guarded the park's left, right, front, and rear gates, preventing pedestrians from passing through. The division headquarters' special service company was also fully mobilized. It was originally hoped that the firearms of the team would be confiscated, and after training by personnel dispatched by the division headquarters, they would be re-assigned. At around 11 a.m., Regiment Commander Du addressed all the team members, ultimately urging them to abide by discipline and obey orders. He also recounted the various complaints against each team, and announced that he was now ordered to have each team submit their firearms for verification, and personnel would be dispatched for training. Unexpectedly, the soldiers of each team disobeyed. During Regiment Commander Du's address, they each loaded their guns with bullets, preparing to resist. Commander Du remained calm, ordering them not to load bullets and summoning the three team leaders to the front for earnest persuasion, ordering the three team leaders to order their teams to turn in their guns. Unexpectedly, the three team leaders refused and loudly protested. At that time, following behind the three team leaders were a platoon leader and a soldier from the 478th Regiment, both armed and monitoring them. When Zheng and others loudly protested, the team soldiers heard from afar, and also shouted and killed, and each used their guns to fire at the 478th Regiment soldiers behind them, and try to escape. The 478th Regiment soldiers immediately scattered and returned fire. Suddenly, the sounds of gunfire boomed, and the city residents fled in alarm, shops closed, and the main roads of the city were temporarily under curfew. As a result, besides those killed on the spot, the rest escaped over the short walls of the park, fleeing into the civilian houses in the Lianzi Street and Xiehe Road area. The army split up to search for them. A rebel soldier ran into the Chen Gui house at 16 Lianzi Street, where Chen's father and wife were. When the army arrived, they ordered them to escape quickly in order to open fire, but the two trembled and could not move. The rebel soldier took the opportunity to open fire, and the army swept with submachine guns, finally killing him. Chen's father was shot in the foot and his wife in the leg. Also, one soldier was killed in an empty house at No. 36. By a little after 12 o'clock, it finally settled down. Inside and outside the park were filled with corpses bathed in blood. Afterwards, it was determined that those killed on the spot included First Team Leader Zheng Yuanlong, Second Team Leader Hong Haojie, and squad leaders and soldiers Feng Tianshui, Zhang Dabao, Xu Qisheng, Wang Jiao, Xu Shuilong, Hong Shuisheng, Hong Mingyuan, Zheng Qiwen, Yan Lintian, Feng Ren, Zhang Ou, Zhang Jinshou, Chen Baishui, Zheng Rengen, Chen Sun, Hong Jinming, Zheng Shishi.

Hong Taishan, Huang Shuihe, Huang Buyong, Su Mao, Wang Xiaotiao, Hong Aidu, Chen Jianqiu, Lu Jinzhang, Hong Shuimu, Zheng Chun, Feng Tianxing, Zheng Hui, Zhang Ji, Zhang Bu, Huang Laogen. In addition, there are five corpses whose names are unknown. The above total is 39 killed.
